***равняться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:равняться.html>равня́ться</a> (13356)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:равнять.html>равня́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ravnjátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:равняться.html>равня́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ravnjátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сравняться.html>сравня́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to compete, to match
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:никто.html>никто́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мочь.html>мо́жет</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:равняться.html>равня́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ним</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">niktó ne móžet <b>ravnjátʹsja</b> s nim</i> ― <span class="e-translation">nobody can compete with him, he is without a rival</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to be equal, to be equivalent, to amount
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дважды.html>два́жды</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:три.html>три</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:равняться.html>равня́ется</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:шесть.html>шести́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">dváždy tri <b>ravnjájetsja</b> šestí</i> ― <span class="e-translation">twice three makes six</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to emulate, to follow the example
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:равняться.html>равня́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лучший.html>лу́чшим</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ravnjátʹsja</b> po lúčšim</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to attain to the level of the best</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">military</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to dress, to align oneself</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:равнять.html>равня́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ravnjátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***рада.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:рада.html>ра́да</a> (1372)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv"><a href = vnd.unilang:рада.html>ра́да</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rada</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle High German">Middle High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh">rât</i> via <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">rada</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Czech_language" class="extiw" title="w:Czech language">Czech</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cs">rada</i>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*rēdaz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рада.html>ра́да</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ráda</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рада.html>ра́ды</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рада.html>ра́ды</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рада.html>ра́д</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>rada, Rada <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">a parliamentary body in a number of Slavic countries</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***ради.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ради.html>ра́ди</a> (948)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Preposition_2">Preposition</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ради.html>ра́ди</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rádi</span>) <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">+ genitive case</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
</p>
<ol><li>for the sake of
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ради.html>ра́ди</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>меня́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>rádi</b> menjá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">for my sake</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ради.html>ра́ди</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ребенок.html>дете́й</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>rádi</b> detéj</i> ― <span class="e-translation">for the sake of the children</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3><p>
The word can be used as both preposition, as in </p><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ради.html>ра́ди</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>меня́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>rádi</b> menjá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">for my sake</span></div><p>, and postposition, as in </p><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бог.html>бо́га</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ради.html>ра́ди</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Bóga <b>rádi</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">for God's sake</span></div><p>. The latter usage tends to be more phrasal.
</p><hr />

<p>Perhaps borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">radial</i> or <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">radial</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:радиальный.html>радиа́льный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">radiálʹnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)радиа́льнее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)радиа́льней</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>radial
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:радиальный.html>радиа́льная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:симметрия.html>симме́трия</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>radiálʹnaja</b> simmétrija</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>radial</b> symmetry</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:радовать.html>ра́довать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rádovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:радоваться.html>ра́доваться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rádovatʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обрадоваться.html>обра́доваться</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:порадоваться.html>пора́доваться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to rejoice, to be glad, to be happy

<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:радовать.html>ра́довать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rádovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***радостно.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:радостно.html>ра́достно</a> (2196)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:радостный.html>ра́достный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rádostnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:радостно.html>ра́достно</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rádostno</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>joyfully, gladly, joyously</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:радость.html>ра́дость</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">rádostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отрада.html>отра́да</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">otráda</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рада.html>ра́д</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">rad</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:радостный.html>ра́достный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">rádostnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отрадный.html>отра́дный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">otrádnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:радовать.html>ра́довать</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">rádovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:радоваться.html>ра́доваться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">rádovatʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возрадоваться.html>возра́доваться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vozradovatʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:порадовать.html>пора́довать</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">porádovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нарадоваться.html>нара́доваться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">naradovatʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:радостно.html>ра́достно</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rádostno</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">short neuter singular of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:радостный.html>ра́достный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rádostnyj</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">joyful, glad, joyous</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***радостный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:радостный.html>ра́достный</a> (2985)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:радость.html>ра́дость</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rádostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Belarusian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Belarusian language">Belarusian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="be">ра́дасны</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="be-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rádasny</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:радостный.html>ра́достный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rádostnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)ра́достнее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)ра́достней</b>)
</p>

***радость.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:радость.html>ра́дость</a> (864)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рада.html>ра́д</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rad</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ость</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:радость.html>ра́дость</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rádostʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:радость.html>ра́дости</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:радость.html>ра́дости</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:радость.html>ра́достей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>joy, delight
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:испуг.html>испу́г</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сменяться.html>сменя́ется</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:радость.html>ра́достью</a></b>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ispúg smenjájetsja <b>rádostʹju</b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Fear turns to <b>joy</b>.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:испуг.html>испу́г</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:смениться.html>смени́лся</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:радость.html>ра́достью</a></b>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ispúg smenílsja <b>rádostʹju</b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Fear turned to <b>joy</b>.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***радужный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:радужный.html>ра́дужный</a> (8090)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:радуга.html>ра́дуг</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rádug</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:радужный.html>ра́дужный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rádužnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)ра́дужнее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)ра́дужней</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> rainbow
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:радужный.html>ра́дужная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:форель.html>форе́ль</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>rádužnaja</b> forɛ́lʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">rainbow trout</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:радужный.html>ра́дужная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:оболочка.html>оболо́чка</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>rádužnaja</b> obolóčka</i> ― <span class="e-translation">iris</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>cheerful
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>него́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:радужный.html>ра́дужное</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:настроение.html>настрое́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">u nevó <b>rádužnoje</b> nastrojénije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he is in very high spirits</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>optimistic, bright, roseate, rosy
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:радужный.html>ра́дужные</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:надежда.html>наде́жды</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>rádužnyje</b> nadéždy</i> ― <span class="e-translation">optimistic expectations</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:радужный.html>ра́дужные</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ожидание.html>ожида́ния</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:предвкушение.html>предвкуше́ния</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>rádužnyje</b> ožidánija/predvkušénija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">rosy anticipations</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:видеть.html>ви́деть</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:представлять.html>представля́ть</a> что́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:радужный.html>ра́дужном</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:свет.html>све́те</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vídetʹ/predstavljátʹ štó-libo v <b>rádužnom</b> svéte</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to have a radiant/glowing picture of something</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рада.html>ра́д</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rad</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-у́шие</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-úšije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:радуший.html>раду́шие</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">radúšije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:радуший.html>раду́шия</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:радуший.html>раду́шия</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:радуший.html>раду́ший</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>cordiality, kindliness, hospitality</li></ol>
